dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Antivirus Compatibility &amp; Known False Positives</h1><a id="user-content-antivirus-compatibility--known-false-positives" <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🚨 Bitdefender False Positive - RestrictRemoteSAM</h2><a id="user-content--bitdefender-false-positive---restrictremotesam" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🚨 Bitdefender False Positive - RestrictRemoteSAM" href="#-bitdefender-false-positive---restrictremotesam"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue Summary</h3><a id="user-content-issue-summary" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue Summary" href="#issue-summary"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Detection:</strong> <code>Heur.BZC.Boxter.151.7C4B21F2</code><br>
<strong>Affected Registry Key:</strong> <code>HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Lsa\RestrictRemoteSAM</code><br>
<strong>Status:</strong> ✅ <strong>FALSE POSITIVE</strong> - This is a legitimate Microsoft Security Baseline policy</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What Happened?</h3><a id="user-content-what-happened" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What Happened?" href="#what-happened"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Bitdefender may flag the <code>RestrictRemoteSAM</code> registry key as malicious during or after running the security baseline script. This is a <strong>FALSE POSITIVE</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Typical Scenario:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>User runs <code>Apply-Win11-25H2-SecurityBaseline.ps1</code></li>
<li>Script sets <code>RestrictRemoteSAM</code> (Microsoft Security Baseline 25H2 policy)</li>
<li>Later: User installs drivers or updates (e.g., Intel Arc drivers)</li>
<li>Bitdefender scans during installation → Detects <code>RestrictRemoteSAM</code> → Blocks process</li>
<li>Installation fails or requires manual intervention</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why Is This Happening?</h3><a id="user-content-why-is-this-happening" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why Is This Happening?" href="#why-is-this-happening"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Bitdefender's Logic (Incorrect):</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Malware → Manipulates SAM Database → Steals Credentials
Our Script → Sets RestrictRemoteSAM → Bitdefender thinks: &quot;Malware!&quot; ❌"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Malware → Manipulates SAM Database → Steals Credentials
Our Script → Sets RestrictRemoteSAM → Bitdefender thinks: "Malware!" ❌
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Reality:</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Our Script → Sets RestrictRemoteSAM → PROTECTS against malware ✅
Microsoft Security Baseline 25H2 → REQUIRES this key ✅"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Our Script → Sets RestrictRemoteSAM → PROTECTS against malware ✅
Microsoft Security Baseline 25H2 → REQUIRES this key ✅
</code></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Is RestrictRemoteSAM Safe?</h3><a id="user-content-is-restrictremotesam-safe" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Is RestrictRemoteSAM Safe?" href="#is-restrictremotesam-safe"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>YES! 100% LEGITIMATE AND RECOMMENDED BY MICROSOFT!</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>What This Key Does:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Purpose:</strong> Restricts remote access to the Security Accounts Manager (SAM) database</li>
<li><strong>Value:</strong> <code>O:BAG:BAD:(A;;RC;;;BA)</code> (SDDL format)</li>
<li><strong>Translation:</strong> Only Administrators can make remote SAM queries</li>
<li><strong>Protection:</strong> Prevents Pass-the-Hash attacks, credential dumping, lateral movement</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Official Sources:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Microsoft Security Baseline 25H2</strong> - Required</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Policy Name:</strong> "Network access: Restrict clients allowed to make remote calls to SAM"</li>
<li>✅ <strong>CIS Benchmark</strong> - Recommended</li>
<li>✅ <strong>DoD STIG</strong> - Required for government systems</li>
<li>✅ <strong>NIST 800-53</strong> - Security control AC-3</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Security Benefits:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ Blocks Pass-the-Hash (PtH) attacks</li>
<li>✅ Prevents remote credential dumping</li>
<li>✅ Stops SAM database enumeration</li>
<li>✅ Mitigates lateral movement in networks</li>
<li>✅ Protects against Mimikatz-style attacks</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Code Reference:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# SecurityBaseline-Core.ps1, Line 1473-1474
Set-RegistryValue -Path &quot;HKLM:\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Lsa&quot; 
                  -Name &quot;RestrictRemoteSAM&quot; 
                  -Value &quot;O:BAG:BAD:(A;;RC;;;BA)&quot; 
                  -Type String"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> SecurityBaseline-Core.ps1, Line 1473-1474</span>
<span class="pl-c1">Set-RegistryValue</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HKLM:\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Lsa<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 
                  <span class="pl-k">-</span>Name <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>RestrictRemoteSAM<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 
                  <span class="pl-k">-</span>Value <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>O:BAG:BAD:(A;;RC;;;BA)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 
                  <span class="pl-k">-</span>Type String</pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> DO NOT REMOVE THIS KEY!</h2><a id="user-content-️-do-not-remove-this-key" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ⚠️ DO NOT REMOVE THIS KEY!" href="#️-do-not-remove-this-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Removing <code>RestrictRemoteSAM</code> would:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>❌ Make your system LESS secure</li>
<li>❌ Enable Pass-the-Hash attacks</li>
<li>❌ Allow credential theft</li>
<li>❌ Violate Microsoft Security Baseline</li>
<li>❌ Fail compliance checks (CIS, STIG, NIST)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>The correct solution is to whitelist the key in Bitdefender, NOT remove it!</strong></p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔧 Solution: Bitdefender Whitelist</h2><a id="user-content--solution-bitdefender-whitelist" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔧 Solution: Bitdefender Whitelist" href="#-solution-bitdefender-whitelist"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Method 1: Registry Exclusion (Recommended)</h3><a id="user-content-method-1-registry-exclusion-recommended" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Method 1: Registry Exclusion (Recommended)" href="#method-1-registry-exclusion-recommended"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Steps:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Open <strong>Bitdefender</strong></li>
<li>Navigate to: <strong>Protection</strong> → <strong>Vulnerability</strong> → <strong>Settings</strong></li>
<li>Scroll to: <strong>Exclusions</strong></li>
<li>Click: <strong>Add Exclusion</strong></li>
<li>Select: <strong>Registry Key</strong></li>
<li>Enter: <code>HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Lsa\RestrictRemoteSAM</code></li>
<li>Add note: "Microsoft Security Baseline 25H2 - Anti-Malware Policy"</li>
<li>Click: <strong>Save</strong></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Screenshot Path:</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Bitdefender → Protection → Vulnerability → Settings → Exclusions → Add Exclusion"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Bitdefender → Protection → Vulnerability → Settings → Exclusions → Add Exclusion
</code></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Method 2: Script Exclusion</h3><a id="user-content-method-2-script-exclusion" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Method 2: Script Exclusion" href="#method-2-script-exclusion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>If Method 1 doesn't work, exclude the entire script:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Steps:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Open <strong>Bitdefender</strong></li>
<li>Navigate to: <strong>Protection</strong> → <strong>Antivirus</strong> → <strong>Settings</strong></li>
<li>Scroll to: <strong>Exclusions</strong></li>
<li>Click: <strong>Add Exclusion</strong></li>
<li>Select: <strong>File or Folder</strong></li>
<li>Browse to: <code>C:\Users\[YourUsername]\...\windsurf-project\Apply-Win11-25H2-SecurityBaseline.ps1</code></li>
<li>Add note: "NoID Privacy - Microsoft Security Baseline Script"</li>
<li>Click: <strong>Save</strong></li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Method 3: Report False Positive to Bitdefender</h3><a id="user-content-method-3-report-false-positive-to-bitdefender" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Method 3: Report False Positive to Bitdefender" href="#method-3-report-false-positive-to-bitdefender"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Help Bitdefender improve their detection:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Visit: <a href="https://www.bitdefender.com/consumer/support/answer/29358/" rel="nofollow">https://www.bitdefender.com/consumer/support/answer/29358/</a></li>
<li>Select: <strong>False Positive Report</strong></li>
<li>Provide:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>File/Script:</strong> <code>Apply-Win11-25H2-SecurityBaseline.ps1</code></li>
<li><strong>Detection Name:</strong> <code>Heur.BZC.Boxter.151.7C4B21F2</code></li>
<li><strong>Registry Key:</strong> <code>RestrictRemoteSAM</code></li>
<li><strong>Explanation:</strong> "False positive - This is a legitimate Microsoft Security Baseline 25H2 policy (Network access: Restrict clients allowed to make remote calls to SAM). The key PROTECTS against credential theft and Pass-the-Hash attacks. Official Microsoft documentation: <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/security/threat-protection/security-policy-settings/network-access-restrict-clients-allowed-to-make-remote-sam-calls" rel="nofollow">https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/security/threat-protection/security-policy-settings/network-access-restrict-clients-allowed-to-make-remote-sam-calls</a>"</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Submit</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>This helps Bitdefender fix their heuristics!</strong></p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📊 Impact on Other Software</h2><a id="user-content--impact-on-other-software" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📊 Impact on Other Software" href="#-impact-on-other-software"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Affected Scenarios:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Driver Installations</strong> (Intel, NVIDIA, AMD) - May be blocked during PowerShell integrity checks</li>
<li>✅ <strong>System Updates</strong> - May trigger false positive during update process</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Software Installers</strong> - Any installer using PowerShell + registry checks</li>
<li>✅ <strong>IT Management Tools</strong> - SCCM, Intune, PDQ Deploy scripts</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example - Intel Driver Installation Failure:</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="1. Intel installer starts
2. Extracts files to %TEMP%
3. Tries to launch driver installer from %TEMP%
4. → Bitdefender blocks! (RestrictRemoteSAM false positive)
5. Installation fails with error"><pre class="notranslate"><code>1. Intel installer starts
2. Extracts files to %TEMP%
3. Tries to launch driver installer from %TEMP%
4. → Bitdefender blocks! (RestrictRemoteSAM false positive)
5. Installation fails with error
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Workarounds:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Method 1: Manual Installation from Desktop (Recommended)</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Run Intel installer (it extracts to <code>%TEMP%</code>)</li>
<li>Installation will fail (Bitdefender blocks)</li>
<li>Go to: <code>C:\Users\[YourUsername]\AppData\Local\Temp\</code></li>
<li>Find Intel extracted folder (e.g., <code>Intel_Graphics_...</code>)</li>
<li>Copy entire folder to Desktop</li>
<li>Run installer from Desktop → Works! ✅</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Method 2: Temporary Disable Protection</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Disable Bitdefender protection during installation</li>
<li>Re-enable after installation completes</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Method 3: Add Exclusion First</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Add <code>RestrictRemoteSAM</code> registry key to exclusions (see above)</li>
<li>Then run Intel installer normally</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🛡️ Third-Party Antivirus &amp; Microsoft Defender Integration</h2><a id="user-content-️-third-party-antivirus--microsoft-defender-integration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🛡️ Third-Party Antivirus &amp; Microsoft Defender Integration" href="#️-third-party-antivirus--microsoft-defender-integration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h3><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Important:</strong> Third-party antivirus products (Bitdefender, Kaspersky, Norton, etc.) <strong>replace</strong> Windows Defender when installed. This affects certain script features and Verify results.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What Happens When Third-Party AV is Installed?</h3><a id="user-content-what-happens-when-third-party-av-is-installed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What Happens When Third-Party AV is Installed?" href="#what-happens-when-third-party-av-is-installed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Windows Defender Status:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Real-Time Protection:</strong> Disabled (third-party AV takes over)</li>
<li>✅ <strong>PowerShell Cmdlets:</strong> May fail or return <code>$null</code></li>
<li>✅ <strong>Registry Keys:</strong> May not be set</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Features:</strong> Replaced by third-party AV equivalents</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Affected PowerShell Cmdlets:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Get-MpPreference     # Returns $null or fails
Set-MpPreference     # Fails or has no effect
Get-MpComputerStatus # Returns inactive status"><pre><span class="pl-c1">Get-MpPreference</span>     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Returns $null or fails</span>
<span class="pl-c1">Set-MpPreference</span>     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Fails or has no effect</span>
<span class="pl-c1">Get-MpComputerStatus</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Returns inactive status</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔍 Impact on Apply Script</h3><a id="user-content--impact-on-apply-script" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔍 Impact on Apply Script" href="#-impact-on-apply-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📊 Impact on Verify Script</h3><a id="user-content--impact-on-verify-script" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📊 Impact on Verify Script" href="#-impact-on-verify-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Failed Checks on Third-Party AV Systems:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>❌ 19x ASR Rules (all rules)</li>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Why This Is OK:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ Third-party AV provides <strong>equivalent or better</strong> protection</li>
<li>✅ ASR → Replaced by AV's exploit prevention</li>
<li>✅ Network Protection → Replaced by AV's web filtering</li>
<li>✅ Cloud Protection → Replaced by AV's cloud scanning</li>
<li>✅ Your system is <strong>still fully protected</strong>!</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example - Bitdefender Equivalents:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ASR Rules → <strong>Advanced Threat Defense</strong></li>
<li>Network Protection → <strong>Web Filtering + Anti-Phishing</strong></li>
<li>Cloud Protection → <strong>Cloud-based Scanning</strong></li>
<li>Controlled Folder Access → <strong>Ransomware Remediation</strong></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example - Kaspersky Equivalents:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ASR Rules → <strong>Exploit Prevention + HIPS</strong></li>
<li>Network Protection → <strong>Web Anti-Virus</strong></li>
<li>Cloud Protection → <strong>Kaspersky Security Network</strong></li>
<li>Controlled Folder Access → <strong>Anti-Ransomware</strong></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> Common Third-Party AV Products</h3><a id="user-content-️-common-third-party-av-products" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ⚠️ Common Third-Party AV Products" href="#️-common-third-party-av-products"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Tested &amp; Working (with expected Verify differences):</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Bitdefender</strong> - 98/121 PASS (RestrictRemoteSAM false positive, see above)</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Kaspersky</strong> - ~100/121 PASS (Defender features unavailable)</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Norton/Symantec</strong> - ~100/121 PASS (may flag script, add to exclusions)</li>
<li>✅ <strong>ESET NOD32</strong> - ~100/121 PASS (Defender features unavailable)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>May Work (Not Fully Tested):</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> <strong>Avast/AVG</strong> - May flag PowerShell execution</li>
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> <strong>McAfee</strong> - Unknown compatibility</li>
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> <strong>Trend Micro</strong> - Unknown compatibility</li>
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> <strong>F-Secure</strong> - Unknown compatibility</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Native Defender Only:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Windows Defender</strong> (Microsoft) - 120/121 PASS</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔧 How to Check What's Protecting You</h3><a id="user-content--how-to-check-whats-protecting-you" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔧 How to Check What's Protecting You" href="#-how-to-check-whats-protecting-you"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>PowerShell Command:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Check Defender status
Get-MpComputerStatus | Select-Object AntivirusEnabled, RealTimeProtectionEnabled

# If this fails or shows &quot;False&quot; → Third-party AV is active"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Check Defender status</span>
<span class="pl-c1">Get-MpComputerStatus</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">Select-Object</span> AntivirusEnabled<span class="pl-k">,</span> RealTimeProtectionEnabled

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> If this fails or shows "False" → Third-party AV is active</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Alternative (Registry):</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Check for third-party AV
Get-CimInstance -Namespace root/SecurityCenter2 -ClassName AntivirusProduct |
    Select-Object displayName, productState"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Check for third-party AV</span>
<span class="pl-c1">Get-CimInstance</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Namespace root<span class="pl-k">/</span>SecurityCenter2 <span class="pl-k">-</span>ClassName AntivirusProduct <span class="pl-k">|</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">Select-Object</span> displayName<span class="pl-k">,</span> productState</pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">💡 Recommendations</h3><a id="user-content--recommendations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 💡 Recommendations" href="#-recommendations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>If You Use Third-Party AV:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Run the script anyway!</strong> - 99% of hardening still works</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Check your AV's settings</strong> - Enable equivalents:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Exploit Prevention / ASR-like features</li>
<li>Web Filtering / Network Protection</li>
<li>Cloud Scanning / Reputation</li>
<li>Ransomware Protection / Controlled Folders</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Verify results: 98-102/121 PASS is excellent!</strong></li>
<li>✅ <strong>Don't worry about Defender fails</strong> - Your AV provides protection</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>If You Want 120/121 PASS:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Uninstall third-party AV</li>
<li>Use native Windows Defender (excellent protection!)</li>
<li>Re-run the script</li>
<li>Verify: Should show 120/121 PASS</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">May Require Exclusions</h3><a id="user-content-may-require-exclusions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: May Require Exclusions" href="#may-require-exclusions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> <strong>Norton/Symantec</strong> - May flag registry modifications (add script to exclusions)</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔍 How to Verify the Key is Safe</h2><a id="user-content--how-to-verify-the-key-is-safe" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔍 How to Verify the Key is Safe" href="#-how-to-verify-the-key-is-safe"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Check the key yourself:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Open PowerShell as Administrator
Get-ItemProperty -Path &quot;HKLM:\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Lsa&quot; -Name &quot;RestrictRemoteSAM&quot;

# Expected Output:
# RestrictRemoteSAM : O:BAG:BAD:(A;;RC;;;BA)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Open PowerShell as Administrator</span>
<span class="pl-c1">Get-ItemProperty</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HKLM:\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Lsa<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Name <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>RestrictRemoteSAM<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Expected Output:</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> RestrictRemoteSAM : O:BAG:BAD:(A;;RC;;;BA)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Decode the SDDL:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="ConvertFrom-SddlString -Sddl &quot;O:BAG:BAD:(A;;RC;;;BA)&quot;

# Output shows:
# Owner: BUILTIN\Administrators
# Group: BUILTIN\Administrators
# Access: Allow Read Control to BUILTIN\Administrators"><pre><span class="pl-c1">ConvertFrom-SddlString</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Sddl <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>O:BAG:BAD:(A;;RC;;;BA)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Output shows:</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Owner: BUILTIN\Administrators</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Group: BUILTIN\Administrators</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Access: Allow Read Control to BUILTIN\Administrators</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Translation:</strong> Only Administrators can read/query the SAM database remotely. This is GOOD security!</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📚 References</h2><a id="user-content--references" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📚 References" href="#-references"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Official Microsoft Documentation</h3><a id="user-content-official-microsoft-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Official Microsoft Documentation" href="#official-microsoft-documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Policy Documentation:</strong> <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/security/threat-protection/security-policy-settings/network-access-restrict-clients-allowed-to-make-remote-sam-calls" rel="nofollow">https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/security/threat-protection/security-policy-settings/network-access-restrict-clients-allowed-to-make-remote-sam-calls</a></li>
<li><strong>Microsoft Security Baseline 25H2:</strong> <a href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=55319" rel="nofollow">https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=55319</a></li>
<li><strong>Group Policy Reference:</strong> <a href="https://admx.help/?Category=Windows_11_2022&amp;Policy=Microsoft.Policies.CredSsp::RestrictRemoteSAM" rel="nofollow">https://admx.help/?Category=Windows_11_2022&amp;Policy=Microsoft.Policies.CredSsp::RestrictRemoteSAM</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Security Standards</h3><a id="user-content-security-standards" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Security Standards" href="#security-standards"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>CIS Benchmark Windows 11:</strong> Section 2.3.10.9</li>
<li><strong>DoD STIG Windows 11:</strong> V-253260</li>
<li><strong>NIST 800-53 Rev 5:</strong> AC-3 (Access Enforcement)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technical Resources</h3><a id="user-content-technical-resources" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technical Resources" href="#technical-resources"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>SDDL Format:</strong> <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/win32/secauthz/security-descriptor-string-format" rel="nofollow">https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/win32/secauthz/security-descriptor-string-format</a></li>
<li><strong>SAM Database Security:</strong> <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows-server/security/credentials-protection-and-management/configuring-additional-lsa-protection" rel="nofollow">https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows-server/security/credentials-protection-and-management/configuring-additional-lsa-protection</a></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">💬 Support</h2><a id="user-content--support" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 💬 Support" href="#-support"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>If you still have concerns:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>✅ Check the official Microsoft documentation links above</li>
<li>✅ Verify the key value matches Microsoft's recommendation</li>
<li>✅ Review our code: <code>Modules\SecurityBaseline-Core.ps1</code> (Line 1473-1474)</li>
<li>✅ Open an issue on GitHub with your antivirus logs</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Remember:</strong> This is a FALSE POSITIVE. The key is PROTECTING you, not attacking you!</p>
